 1967 ke baad hue chunaavon main revolutionari socialist party kaa zyaadaatar samay yahaan danka bajataa rahaa he

 farji tiiti shikshakon ko galat tareekon se karodon rupayon ke vetan bhugtan karne ke maamle ko mujffarpur court ne gambhirtha purvak lete hue yah faisla sunaaya he
 Muzaffarpur CJM Court, Principal Secretary of Education Department R
 ke
 Nagar Thana has been ordered to file a lawsuit under section 409,465,468,471,120B and section 420 of IPC on more than two dozen officers including Mahajan
 galit tareeke se bhugtan kaa he maamalamujaffarpur jile ke vibhinn prakhandon main jaanch ke dauraan paaya gaya ki 335 tiiti shikshakon kii farji tareeke se niyukti kii gayi
 In spite of this, the salary was paid by the fake teachers department without matching the cds received from the officials of the Education Department
 farji tiiti shikshakon ko galat tareeke se vetan bhugtan karne ke babat pankaj kumaar adhivaktaa ne mujffarpur vyavhaar nyaayalay main pariwaad patr daayar kiya tha
 While hearing the same matter, the Chief Judicial Magistrate of Muzaffarpur Behavior Court ordered to register the case
 in sabake bichmujaffarpurake jiladhikari ne bhi farji shikshakon ko galat tareeke se vetan bhugtan kiye jane ke maamle ko lekar isaki sangyaan maanga he
 According to the information, 9 fake TET teachers were identified in Paru 9, 35 in Bochan, 6 in Sakra, 9 in Motipur, 22 in Saraiya, 6 in Kanti, 26 in Gaighat, 16 in Mushahari, 145 in Meenapur and 61 in Bandra
 
 jabaki aurai, murul, katra, madwan, kudhani sahibganj or nagar thana kshetra ke shiksha adhikari ne abhi tak report nahin saunpi he
 The District Magistrate has demanded detailed information in this matter from the DPO so that further action can be taken

 Both films have received four nominations
 shahrukh khan-kaajol kii 'dilavaale' ko teen namakan mili hai, jinamein badtar film, badtar nirdeshak (rohit shetty) or sabase dukhadaayi gaanaa (gerua) shaamil he

 Some telecom companies of India have started 4G service in India
 4G yani 4th jenereshan mobile telecommunication technology
 Currently, Airtel and Aircel have launched 4G service in about a dozen cities across the country, including most major cities including Delhi and Mumbai
 ham bataate hai bharat main kaisaa hoga 4G sarvice or isse ek aam mobile phone yuzar par kya fark padegaa
 How will 4G be compared to 3G 4G will be 4 times faster than 4G3G
 abhi 3G main 21mbps kii speed milti he 4G main 100mbps kii speed milegi
 However, in India, mobile companies offer inferior service in the name of 3G service
 agar sahi myne main mobile companiyaan 4G sarvice prowide karen to 3G par jis gane ko downlod karne main aapako agar 8 second lagate hai to 4G main yahi gaanaa 2 second se bhi kam main downlod ho jayega
 The video you see on the ordinary Internet now stops quite intermittently

 To avail 4G service from a mobile company, you must have a smartphone with 4G technology

 1
 To clean the microwave, cut lemon pieces in a cup of water and keep it in the microwave to heat up for 15 minutes

 2
 To remove the stench from the litter box, add lemon juice to it and then wash it with cold water
 3
 Rubbing a piece of lemon on the vegetable cutting chopping board to remove fruit and vegetable stains will remove both the stain and the smell of the vegetable

 To remove stains from clothes, rub a piece of lemon on that stain and then wash it and dry it in the sun

 ab jin rajyon main chunaav hone vaale hai, vahaan bijepi ne puri tarah se vipaksh kaa safaya kar diya tha
 In the third phase, polling will be held in 26 Lok Sabha seats in Gujarat, the home state of Prime Minister Narendra Modi and BJP President Amit Shah
 2014 main bijepi yahaan kii sabhi siten jeetne main kaamyaab rahi thi, aise main is baar ke chunaav main party ke saamne in siton ko bachaae rakhane kii badi chunauti he
 Apart from this, voting has been done for 14 seats out of 28 seats in Karnataka, votes will be cast on April 23 for the remaining 14 seats
 2014 main bijepi 17 siten jeetne main safal rahi thi
 In this way, the third phase is very important for BJP, BJP had 11 out of 14 seats
 madhya pradesh kii 29 siton par aakhri ke chaar charnon main chunaav hone hai
 The BJP was successful in winning 27 seats in the last election
 haal hi main hue vidhansabha chunaav main bijepi ko maat dekar congress satta main vaapasi kii he
 In such a situation, it is a tough challenge for the BJP to retain their seats
 iske alaava rajasthan kii 25 siton par chauthe or paanchave charan main voting honi he
 The BJP was successful in winning all the seats in the 2014 Lok Sabha elections
 madhya pradesh kii tarah hi rajasthan main bhi bijepi ko maat dekar congress satta main ai he
 In such a situation, it is not easy for BJP to repeat the victory in these seats
 uttar pradesh kii 80 loksabhaa siton main se 16 siton par chunaav ho chuke hai, baaki bachi 64 siton par aagaamee paanch charnon main voting hogi
